<section type="Title-page">
&#182; <term lang="la">Sex linguar<expan type="">um</expan> / Latine / Teu&#173;
thonice, Gallice, Hispanice, Italice,
Anglice, dilucidissimus dictionarius, mirum <expan type="">que</expan> v&#173;
tilis, ne dicam necessarius omnibus, lin&#173;
guarum studiosis.</term>
&#182; <term lang="ge">Vocabulaer in sesterley talen, La&#173;
tyn, Duytsch, Walsch, Spaens, Italiaens, &#38; En&#38;shy
gelsch, seer profitelick alle beminders
der talen.</term>
&#182; <term lang="fr">Vocabulaire de six languages, La&#38;shy
tin, Flameng, Francoys, Espaignol, Italien,
et Anglois.</term>
&#182; <term lang="sp">Vocabulario de scir languaies, La<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
tin, Flamenco, Frances, Espaignol, Italian,
y Englese.</term>
&#182; <term lang="it">Vocabulista de le sci lingue, Cioe
Latina, Tudescha, Franzosa, S<emend err="s"></emend>pagniola, Ita&#38;shy
liana, &#38; Anglese.</term>
&#182; <term lang="en">A Vocabulary in six languages, La<emend err="">&#173;</emend>
tyn, Dutch, Frenche, Spanish, Italy, and Englysh.</term>

&#182; <term lang="en">Imprynted in Southwarke by me
Iames Nicolson.
1537.</term>

</section>
